\hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source}{}\doxysection{translator.\+py}
\label{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source}\index{doxygen/build/doxygen/doc/translator.py@{doxygen/build/doxygen/doc/translator.py}}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00001}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetranslator}{00001}} \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}"{}"{}Script to generate reports on translator classes from Doxygen sources.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00002}00002 \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00003}00003 \textcolor{stringliteral}{  The main purpose of the script }\textcolor{keywordflow}{is} to extract the information \textcolor{keyword}{from} sources}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00004}00004   related to internationalization (the translator classes). It uses the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00005}00005   information to generate documentation (language.doc,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00006}00006   translator\_report.txt) \textcolor{keyword}{from} templates (language.tpl, maintainers.txt).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00007}00007 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00008}00008   Simply run the script without parameters to get the reports \textcolor{keywordflow}{and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00009}00009   documentation \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} all supported languages. If you want to generate the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00010}00010   translator report only \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} some languages, \textcolor{keywordflow}{pass} their codes \textcolor{keyword}{as} arguments}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00011}00011   to the script. In that case, the language.doc will \textcolor{keywordflow}{not} be generated.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00012}00012   Example:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00013}00013 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00014}00014     python translator.py en nl cz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00015}00015 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00016}00016   Originally, the script was written \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} Perl \textcolor{keywordflow}{and} was known \textcolor{keyword}{as} translator.pl.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00017}00017   The last Perl version was dated 2002/05/21 (plus some later corrections)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2doc_2translator_8py_source_l00018}00018 }
